[1mEXAMPLES[0m[m
       [1mifup[0m [1m-a[0m[m
              Bring  up  all  the  interfaces  defined  with [4mauto[24m in [4m/etc/net‚Äê[24m[m
              [4mwork/interfaces[24m[m
[m
       [1mifup[0m [1meth0[0m[m
              Bring up interface [1meth0[0m[m
[m
       [1mifup[0m [1meth0=home[0m[m
              Bring up interface [1meth0[0m as logical interface [1mhome[0m[m
[m
       [1mifdown[0m [1m-a[0m[m
              Bring down all interfaces that are currently up.[m
[m
       [1mifquery[0m [1m-l[0m[m
              Print names of all interfaces specified with the [1mauto[0m keyword.[m
[m
       [1mifquery[0m [1m-l[0m [1m--allow=hotplug[0m[m
              Print names of all interfaces specified with  the  [1mallow-hotplug[0m[m
              keyword.[m
[m
       [1mifquery[0m [1meth0[0m[m
[7m Manual page ifup(8) line 113 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K[7m Manual page ifup(8) line 113 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K

[K[7mNo previous regular expression  (press RETURN)[27m[24;1H[K
[K              Display  the interface options as specified in the [1mifupdown[0m con‚Äê[m
              figuration. Each key-value pair is  printed  out  on  individual[m
              line using "[1m:[0m " as separator.[m

[1mNOTES[0m[m
       [1mifup[0m,  [1mifdown[0m, and [1mifquery[0m are actually the same program called by dif‚Äê[m
       ferent names.[m
[m
       The program does not configure network interfaces directly; it runs low[m
       level utilities such as [1mip[0m to do its dirty work.[m
[m
       When  invoked,  [1mifdown[0m  checks  if [1mifup[0m is still running. In that case,[m
       [1mSIGTERM[0m is sent to ifup.[m
[m
[1mFILES[0m[m

              definitions of network interfaces  See  [1minterfaces[0m(5)  for  more[m
              information.[m
[m
       [4m/run/network/ifstate[24m[m
              current state of network interfaces[m

[HM[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m

[HM       ifquery - parse interface configuration[m

[K[7m Manual page ifup(8) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K[m
       [1mifquery[0m [1m--state[0m [[4mIFACE[24m...][m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       The  [1mifup[0m  and  [1mifdown[0m  commands  may be used to configure (or, respec‚Äê[m
       tively, deconfigure) network interfaces based on interface  definitions[m
       in  the  file  [4m/etc/network/interfaces[24m.  [1mifquery[0m command may be used to[m
       parse interfaces configuration.[m
[m
[1mOPTIONS[0m[m
       A summary of options is included below.[m
[m
       [1m-a[0m, [1m--all[0m[m
              If given to [1mifup[0m, affect all interfaces marked [1mauto[0m.  Interfaces[m
              are  brought  up  in  the  order  in  which  they are defined in[m
              [4m/etc/network/interfaces[24m.  Combined with  [1m--allow[0m,  acts  on  all[m
              interfaces  of  a  specified class instead.  If given to [1mifdown[0m,[m
              affect all defined interfaces.  Interfaces are brought  down  in[m
              the  order in which they are currently listed in the state file.[m
              Only  interfaces  defined  in  [4m/etc/network/interfaces[24m  will  be[m
              brought down.[m
[m
       [1m--force[0m[m
[7m Manual page ifup(8) line 26 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K              Force configuration or deconfiguration of the interface.[m
[7m Manual page ifup(8) line 27 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K
[K[7mNo next tag  (press RETURN)[27m[24;1H[K
[K...skipping...

      Commands marked with * may be preceded by a number, [4mN[24m.[m
      Notes in parentheses indicate the behavior if [4mN[24m is given.[m
      A key preceded by a caret indicates the Ctrl key; thus ^K is ctrl-K.[m
[m
  h  H                 Display this help.[m
  q  :q  Q  :Q  ZZ     Exit.[m

[m
  e  ^E  j  ^N  CR  *  Forward  one line   (or [4mN[24m lines).[m

  f  ^F  ^V  SPACE  *  Forward  one window (or [4mN[24m lines).[m
  b  ^B  ESC-v      *  Backward one window (or [4mN[24m lines).[m
  z                 *  Forward  one window (and set window to [4mN[24m).[m
  w                 *  Backward one window (and set window to [4mN[24m).[m
  ESC-SPACE         *  Forward  one window, but don't stop at end-of-file.[m
  d  ^D             *  Forward  one half-window (and set half-window to [4mN[24m).[m
  u  ^U             *  Backward one half-window (and set half-window to [4mN[24m).[m
  ESC-)  RightArrow *  Left  one half screen width (or [4mN[24m positions).[m

[K:[K00
[K  ESC-(  LeftArrow  *  Right one half screen width (or [4mN[24m positions).[m

  R                    Repaint screen, discarding buffered input.[m

                          [1mSEARCHING[0m[m
[m
  /[4mpattern[24m          *  Search forward for ([4mN[24m-th) matching line.[m
  ?[4mpattern[24m          *  Search backward for ([4mN[24m-th) matching line.[m
  n                 *  Repeat previous search (for [4mN[24m-th occurrence).[m
  N                 *  Repeat previous search in reverse direction.[m
  ESC-n             *  Repeat previous search, spanning files.[m
  ESC-N             *  Repeat previous search, reverse dir. & spanning files.[m
  ESC-u                Undo (toggle) search highlighting.[m
  &[4mpattern[24m          *  Display only matching lines[m
        ---------------------------------------------------[m
        A search pattern may be preceded by one or more of:[m
        ^N or !  Search for NON-matching lines.[m
        ^E or *  Search multiple files (pass thru END OF FILE).[m
[7mHELP -- Press RETURN for more, or q when done[27m[K
[K:[K11[K99[K22[K..[K11[K66[K88[K..[K00[K..[K22[K00

[K        ^F or @  Start search at FIRST file (for /) or last file (for ?).[m
        ^K       Highlight matches, but don't move (KEEP position).[m

                           [1mJUMPING[0m[m
[m
  g  <  ESC-<       *  Go to first line in file (or line [4mN[24m).[m
  G  >  ESC->       *  Go to last line in file (or line [4mN[24m).[m
  p  %              *  Go to beginning of file (or [4mN[24m percent into file).[m
  t                 *  Go to the ([4mN[24m-th) next tag.[m
  T                 *  Go to the ([4mN[24m-th) previous tag.[m
  {  (  [           *  Find close bracket } ) ].[m
  }  )  ]           *  Find open bracket { ( [.[m
  ESC-^F [4m<c1>[24m [4m<c2>[24m  *  Find close bracket [4m<c2>[24m.[m
  ESC-^B [4m<c1>[24m [4m<c2>[24m  *  Find open bracket [4m<c1>[24m [m
        ---------------------------------------------------[m
        Each "find close bracket" command goes forward to the close bracket [m
          matching the ([4mN[24m-th) open bracket in the top line.[m
        Each "find open bracket" command goes backward to the open bracket [m
          matching the ([4mN[24m-th) close bracket in the bottom line.[m
[m
  m[4m<letter>[24m            Mark the current position with <letter>.[m
  '[4m<letter>[24m            Go to a previously marked position.[m
  ''                   Go to the previous position.[m
  ^X^X                 Same as '.[m
        ---------------------------------------------------[m
        A mark is any upper-case or lower-case letter.[m
        Certain marks are predefined:[m
             ^  means  beginning of the file[m
             $  means  end of the file[m

                           [1mOPTIONS[0m[m
[m
        Most options may be changed either on the command line,[m
        or from within less by using the - or -- command.[m
        Options may be given in one of two forms: either a single[m
        character preceded by a -, or a name preceded by --.[m
[m
  -?  ........  --help[m
                  Display help (from command line).[m
  -a  ........  --search-skip-screen[m
                  Search skips current screen.[m
  -A  ........  --SEARCH-SKIP-SCREEN[m
                  Search starts just after target line.[m
  -b [[4mN[24m]  ....  --buffers=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Number of buffers.[m
  -B  ........  --auto-buffers[m
                  Don't automatically allocate buffers for pipes.[m
  -c  ........  --clear-screen[m
                  Repaint by clearing rather than scrolling.[m
  -d  ........  --dumb[m
                  Dumb terminal.[m
  -D [[4mxn.n[24m]  .  --color=[4mxn.n[24m[m
                  Set screen colors. (MS-DOS only)[m
  -e  -E  ....  --quit-at-eof  --QUIT-AT-EOF[m
                  Quit at end of file.[m
  -f  ........  --force[m
                  Force open non-regular files.[m
  -F  ........  --quit-if-one-screen[m
                  Quit if entire file fits on first screen.[m
  -g  ........  --hilite-search[m
                  Highlight only last match for searches.[m
  -G  ........  --HILITE-SEARCH[m
                  Don't highlight any matches for searches.[m
  -h [[4mN[24m]  ....  --max-back-scroll=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Backward scroll limit.[m
  -i  ........  --ignore-case[m
                  Ignore case in searches that do not contain uppercase.[m
  -I  ........  --IGNORE-CASE[m
                  Ignore case in all searches.[m
  -j [[4mN[24m]  ....  --jump-target=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Screen position of target lines.[m
  -J  ........  --status-column[m
                  Display a status column at left edge of screen.[m
  -k [[4mfile[24m]  .  --lesskey-file=[[4mfile[24m][m
                  Use a lesskey file.[m
  -K            --quit-on-intr[m
                  Exit less in response to ctrl-C.[m
  -L  ........  --no-lessopen[m
                  Ignore the LESSOPEN environment variable.[m
  -m  -M  ....  --long-prompt  --LONG-PROMPT[m
                  Set prompt style.[m
  -n  -N  ....  --line-numbers  --LINE-NUMBERS[m
                  Don't use line numbers.[m
  -o [[4mfile[24m]  .  --log-file=[[4mfile[24m][m
                  Copy to log file (standard input only).[m
  -O [[4mfile[24m]  .  --LOG-FILE=[[4mfile[24m][m
                  Copy to log file (unconditionally overwrite).[m
  -p [[4mpattern[24m]  --pattern=[[4mpattern[24m][m
                  Start at pattern (from command line).[m
  -P [[4mprompt[24m]   --prompt=[[4mprompt[24m][m
                  Define new prompt.[m
  -q  -Q  ....  --quiet  --QUIET  --silent --SILENT[m
                  Quiet the terminal bell.[m
  -r  -R  ....  --raw-control-chars  --RAW-CONTROL-CHARS[m
                  Output "raw" control characters.[m
  -s  ........  --squeeze-blank-lines[m
                  Squeeze multiple blank lines.[m
  -S  ........  --chop-long-lines[m
                  Chop (truncate) long lines rather than wrapping.[m
  -t [[4mtag[24m]  ..  --tag=[[4mtag[24m][m
                  Find a tag.[m
  -T [[4mtagsfile[24m] --tag-file=[[4mtagsfile[24m][m
                  Use an alternate tags file.[m
  -u  -U  ....  --underline-special  --UNDERLINE-SPECIAL[m
                  Change handling of backspaces.[m
  -V  ........  --version[m
                  Display the version number of "less".[m
  -w  ........  --hilite-unread[m
                  Highlight first new line after forward-screen.[m
  -W  ........  --HILITE-UNREAD[m
                  Highlight first new line after any forward movement.[m
  -x [[4mN[24m[,...]]  --tabs=[[4mN[24m[,...]][m
                  Set tab stops.[m
  -X  ........  --no-init[m
                  Don't use termcap init/deinit strings.[m
  -y [[4mN[24m]  ....  --max-forw-scroll=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Forward scroll limit.[m
  -z [[4mN[24m]  ....  --window=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Set size of window.[m
  -" [[4mc[24m[[4mc[24m]]  .  --quotes=[[4mc[24m[[4mc[24m]][m
                  Set shell quote characters.[m
  -~  ........  --tilde[m
                  Don't display tildes after end of file.[m
  -# [[4mN[24m]  ....  --shift=[[4mN[24m][m
                  Horizontal scroll amount (0 = one half screen width)[m
      ........  --no-keypad[m
